# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
The gradient at a particular point of a curve is the gradient of the tangent at that point ^JXONbjrM

the unit or average cost is the cost of producing a certain quantity of product. The marginal
cost is the change in cost of producing an extra ammount of product ^vYf70dW8
